  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然PDDL+语言引入时就已知带持续时间动作的时序规划可以编译为PDDL+，但文献中一直缺乏实用的编译方法

Method: 提出从带持续时间动作的时序规划到PDDL+的实用编译方法，完全捕获语义，仅假设动作非自重叠，编译是多项式复杂度

Result: 编译方法保持计划长度在常数因子内，实验证明对困难的时序数值问题具有实际应用价值

Conclusion: 首次提供了实用的PDDL 2.1到PDDL+编译方法，填补了文献空白，为处理复杂时序数值规划问题提供了有效工具

Abstract: Since the introduction of the PDDL+ modeling language, it was known that temporal planning with durative actions (as in PDDL 2.1) could be compiled into PDDL+. However, no practical compilation was presented in the literature ever since. We present a practical compilation from temporal planning with durative actions into PDDL+, fully capturing the semantics and only assuming the non-self-overlapping of actions. Our compilation is polynomial, retains the plan length up to a constant factor and is experimentally shown to be of practical relevance for hard temporal numeric problems.

</details>


### [182] [Portfolio of Solving Strategies in CEGAR-based Object Packing and Scheduling for Sequential 3D Printing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12224)
*Pavel Surynek*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 并行化CEGAR-SEQ算法用于3D打印对象排列调度，通过多种排列策略组合提升性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代多核个人计算机CPU拥有强大的并行计算能力，可用于解决复杂的组合优化问题，特别是3D打印中的对象排列和调度问题。需要有效利用这些计算资源来改进现有的CEGAR-SEQ算法。

Method: 提出Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ算法，通过并行执行CEGAR-SEQ算法并采用多种对象排列策略组合：1) 将对象放置在打印平台中心（原始策略）；2) 将对象放置在打印平台角落；3) 根据对象高度进行调度。算法将顺序3D打印的对象排列和调度问题表达为线性算术公式，采用基于反例引导抽象精化(CEGAR)的技术求解。

Result: 实验评估表明Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ算法优于原始CEGAR-SEQ算法。在批量对象调度多个打印平台时，Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ通常使用更少的打印平台。

Conclusion: 通过并行化现有算法并采用多种对象排列策略组合，可以有效利用现代多核CPU的计算能力，显著提升3D打印对象排列和调度问题的求解性能，减少所需的打印平台数量。

Abstract: Computing power that used to be available only in supercomputers decades ago especially their parallelism is currently available in standard personal computer CPUs even in CPUs for mobile telephones. We show how to effectively utilize the computing power of modern multi-core personal computer CPU to solve the complex combinatorial problem of object arrangement and scheduling for sequential 3D printing. We achieved this by parallelizing the existing CEGAR-SEQ algorithm that solves the sequential object arrangement and scheduling by expressing it as a linear arithmetic formula which is then solved by a technique inspired by counterexample guided abstraction refinement (CEGAR). The original CEGAR-SEQ algorithm uses an object arrangement strategy that places objects towards the center of the printing plate. We propose alternative object arrangement strategies such as placing objects towards a corner of the printing plate and scheduling objects according to their height. Our parallelization is done at the high-level where we execute the CEGAR-SEQ algorithm in parallel with a portfolio of object arrangement strategies, an algorithm is called Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ. Our experimental evaluation indicates that Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ outperforms the original CEGAR-SEQ. When a batch of objects for multiple printing plates is scheduled, Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ often uses fewer printing plates than CEGAR-SEQ.

</details>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [183] [Towards heterogeneous parallelism for SPHinXsys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11868)
*Xiangyu Hu,Alberto Guarnieri*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出一种弱可压缩光滑粒子流体动力学方法求解两方程雷诺平均Navier-Stokes模型，通过改进的主流区和近壁区处理方法解决了SPH与RANS模型之间的不一致性，首次在SPH-RANS模拟中实现了速度和湍流动能的满意收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决SPH（拉格朗日方法）与RANS模型（基于欧拉框架）在湍流壁面流动中的不一致性问题，特别是强剪切和近壁不连续性导致的数值困难，为粒子方法与网格方法之间的湍流模拟搭建桥梁。

Method: 采用弱可压缩SPH方法求解两方程RANS模型。主流区处理包括自适应黎曼-涡耗散和去噪传输速度公式；近壁区处理包括基于粒子的壁面模型实现、加权近壁补偿方案和恒定壁面法向间距策略；开发基于水平集的边界偏移技术用于收敛测试。

Result: 模拟了直通道、轻度弯曲、强弯曲、半收敛-发散通道和鱼道等多个基准壁面湍流案例，获得了平滑且合理准确的结果，首次在SPH-RANS模拟中实现了速度和湍流动能的满意收敛。

Conclusion: 该方法成功解决了SPH与RANS模型之间的不一致性，为基于粒子和基于网格的RANS模型搭建了桥梁，为其他湍流模型提供了适应性，并为湍流流体-结构相互作用模拟提供了潜力。

Abstract: This paper presents a Weakly Compressible Smoothed Particle Hydrodynamics (WCSPH) method solving the two-equation Reynolds-Averaged Navier-Stokes (RANS) model {for the turbulent wall-bounded flows with or without flow separation. The inconsistency between the Lagrangian nature of the SPH and RANS model, primarily caused by intense shearing and near-wall discontinuities, is firstly revealed and addressed by the improved mainstream and near-wall treatments, respectively.}The mainstream treatments, including Adaptive Riemann-eddy Dissipation (ARD) and { de-noised} transport velocity formulation, address dissipation incompatibility, turbulent kinetic energy disturbance and over-prediction issues. The near-wall treatments, such as the particle-based wall model realization, weighted near-wall compensation scheme, {and constant wall-normal spacing strategy}, improve the accuracy and stability of the adopted wall model, where the wall dummy particles are still used for future coupling of solid dynamics. Besides, to perform rigorous convergence tests, {a level-set-based Boundary-Offset Technique (BOT)} is developed to {ensure consistent wall-normal distance} across different resolutions. Several benchmark wall-bounded turbulent flow cases are simulated, including straight, mildly curved, strongly curved, Half Converging-Diverging (HCD) channels, and a fish-pass. The present method yields smoothed and reasonably accurate results, and, to the best of our knowledge, achieves for the first time satisfactory convergence of both velocity and turbulent kinetic energy in SPH-RANS simulations. The proposed method bridges particle-based and mesh-based RANS models, providing adaptability for other turbulence models and potential for turbulent fluid-structure interaction (FSI) simulations.

</details>
